<a id="p7-24"></a>

### 24 · 용역 입찰 제안 공고, 공급업체의 제안서, 최종 선정 결과 이메일 연계 (삼중 지문)

> 🏷 `삼중지문`  ·  Part 7  ·  CHAPTER 5

**🧭 지문 프레임워크**

> [지문 1: 입찰 공고 RFP] + [지문 2: 입찰 제안서] + [지문 3: 선정 결과 이메일] 삼중 지문 구조입니다.
> · **[지문 1 = 발주처 요구 조건]** 필수 기술 스펙·예산 한도·마감 기한을 명시합니다.
> · **[지문 2 = 공급업체 응찰 내역]** 모듈별 기능·견적 비용·투입 인력을 표로 제시합니다.
> · **[지문 3 = 최종 조율·피드백]** 선정 이유와 옵션 수정 후 최종 계약 조치를 취합니다.
> · **[★삼중 크로스 매칭★]** 지문 2 단가표와 지문 3의 최종 선택을 결합해 실제 계약 금액을 도출합니다.

**📄 지문**

```data
[Passage 1 — Request for Proposals (RFP)]
REQUEST FOR PROPOSALS: REGIONAL DISASTER SAFETY ONTOLOGY PROJECT
Issued By: Jeonbuk Regional Innovation Committee
Release Date: July 1, 2026

The Jeonbuk Regional Innovation Committee is officially soliciting structured proposals from certified technology pioneers to construct a centralized Regional Disaster Safety R&D Platform. This multi-year public sector initiative focuses on synthesizing disparate environmental metadata into a singular dashboard with zero processing latency.

Strict Administrative Controls:
• Mandatory Compliance: All prospective platforms must integrate standard Supabase database architectures pre-configured with secure multi-factor authentication (MFA).
• Financial Constraint: The absolute budget ceiling for the initial implementation phase is strictly capped at $50,000. Under no circumstances will higher bids be reviewed.
• Delivery Deadline: Fully functional algorithmic beta endpoints must be deployed and ready for test simulations no later than August 1.

───

[Passage 2 — Bid Summary Excerpt]
PROJECT BID SUMMARY: PROPOSAL #26-B
SUBMITTED BY: Social Brain AI | Attn: James Albright, COO
DATE OF SUBMISSION: July 8, 2026

DEVELOPMENT MODULES & IMPLEMENTATION FEES
-------------------------------------------------------------------
MODULE CODE | FUNCTIONAL SCOPE                           | BASE LINE COST
-------------------------------------------------------------------
MOD-ONT-01  | Database Ontology Structural Setup         | $25,000
MOD-API-KIS | KIS API Framework Synchronization          | $12,000
MOD-SEC-MFA | Mandatory MFA Portal Implementation       | $8,000
MOD-ANL-PRE | Next-Gen Predictive Analytics (Opt.)       | $10,000
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Auxiliary Add-on: Standard 1-year data cooling server storage warranty: $3,000.

Technical Lead: Sang-wook Ji (Master of Public Administration / 6-year tech lead).

───

[Passage 3 — Email]
From: evaluation-team@jeonbuk-gov.org
To: j.albright@socialbrain-ai.com
Date: July 11, 2026
Subject: Final Selection Result: Proposal #26-B

Dear Mr. Albright,

We are pleased to inform you that the Jeonbuk Regional Innovation Committee has officially selected Social Brain AI as the primary technology vendor for our upcoming Regional Disaster Safety R&D Project based on Proposal #26-B.

Our evaluation panel noted that your team leader, Mr. Ji, possesses an exceptional understanding of B2G administrative structures. Furthermore, your architecture completely satisfies our strict multi-factor authentication mandates with zero processing latency.

To remain perfectly aligned with our financial constraints, please be advised that our committee has approved your proposal excluding the optional predictive analytics module and the auxiliary warranty add-on. We will accept all other foundational modules as originally quoted.

Our procurement team will dispatch the formal binding agreement ledger on Monday. Please ensure your engineering team is fully prepared to commence development immediately so that we can meet our unalterable August 1 deployment deadline.

Sincerely,
Min-ah Song
Project Director, Jeonbuk Regional Innovation Committee
```

**✍️ 실전 예제**

**Q1.** According to the RFP, what is the maximum budget allowed for the initial phase?

- (A) $8,000
- (B) $12,000
- (C) $25,000
- (D) $50,000

> ✅ **정답 · (D) $50,000**
>
> 지문 1 Financial Constraint에 'budget ceiling ... strictly capped at $50,000'이라 나온다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) $8,000 — MFA 모듈 단가다.
> - (B) $12,000 — KIS API 모듈 단가다.
> - (C) $25,000 — 온톨로지 모듈 단가다.
> - **(D) $50,000 — 예산 상한이라 정답.**

**Q2.** What qualification of Social Brain AI's team leader is specifically praised in the email?

- (A) His extensive certification in commercial retail storefront design
- (B) His exceptional understanding of government administrative structures
- (C) His rapid implementation of automated quantitative trading bots
- (D) His background in managing international software licensing disputes

> ✅ **정답 · (B) His exceptional understanding of government administrative structures**
>
> 지문 3에 'Mr. Ji possesses an exceptional understanding of B2G administrative structures'라 나온다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) 상업 소매 매장 설계 자격증 — 칭찬 대상이 아니다.
> - **(B) 정부 행정 구조에 대한 탁월한 이해 — B2G를 치환한 정답.**
> - (C) 자동 퀀트 트레이딩 봇의 신속한 구현 — 칭찬 포인트가 아니다.
> - (D) 국제 소프트웨어 라이선스 분쟁 관리 경력 — 언급되지 않는다.

**Q3.** What was the primary reason Social Brain AI's proposal was eligible for review over other potential over-budget bids?

- (A) Their total baseline cost for all four available modules was exactly $40,000.
- (B) Their maximum possible combination fee including all options was beneath the $50,000 cap.
- (C) They offered a complimentary 1-year data cooling server storage warranty.
- (D) They completed the physical installation of Supabase servers in Seoul.

> ✅ **정답 · (B) Their maximum possible combination fee including all options was beneath the $50,000 cap.**
>
> 지문 1은 상한 $50,000 초과 시 심사에서 제외한다. Social Brain AI의 핵심 이행 모듈(온톨로지 $25,000+KIS API $12,000+MFA $8,000=$45,000)이 상한 아래라 심사 대상이 됐다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) 네 모듈 기본 합이 정확히 $40,000 — 필수 3개 모듈 합은 $45,000이라 수치가 틀렸다.
> - **(B) 예산 상한 $50,000을 넘지 않아 검토 자격 — 상한 이내라 심사된 정답.**
> - (C) 무상 1년 데이터 냉각 워런티 제공 — 워런티는 유상 $3,000이다.
> - (D) 서울에 Supabase 서버 물리 설치 완료 — 그런 언급은 없다.

**Q4.** What will the final total contract price be for the approved project?

- (A) $37,000
- (B) $45,000
- (C) $48,000
- (D) $55,000

> ✅ **정답 · (B) $45,000**
>
> 지문 3에서 옵션 모듈($10,000)과 워런티($3,000)를 제외 승인한다. 지문 2의 남은 모듈 $25,000+$12,000+$8,000=$45,000이다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) $37,000 — 모듈 하나를 더 뺀 오산이다.
> - **(B) $45,000 — 승인된 세 모듈 합이라 정답.**
> - (C) $48,000 — 워런티만 빼고 옵션을 남긴 오산이다.
> - (D) $55,000 — 옵션까지 포함해 승인 범위를 벗어난 금액이다.

**Q5.** What is Social Brain AI expected to do by August 1?

- (A) Submit a revised written proposal with 15% pricing incentives
- (B) Deploy fully functional algorithmic beta endpoints for testing
- (C) Complete a mandatory 14-day training seminar for local staff
- (D) Renew an existing corporate technology consulting agreement

> ✅ **정답 · (B) Deploy fully functional algorithmic beta endpoints for testing**
>
> 지문 1·3 공통으로 '8월 1일까지 fully functional algorithmic beta endpoints를 배치'해야 한다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) 15% 가격 인센티브 담은 수정 제안서 제출 — 그런 요구는 없다.
> - **(B) 테스트용 알고리즘 베타 엔드포인트 배치 — 마감 과업이라 정답.**
> - (C) 지역 직원 대상 14일 교육 세미나 이수 — 언급되지 않는다.
> - (D) 기존 기술 컨설팅 계약 갱신 — 무관하다.

<div align="right"><sub><a href="#part-7">▲ Part 7 · 독해 목차</a></sub></div>

---

<a id="p7-25"></a>

### 25 · 제품 결함 불만 접수, 기술 리포트, 최종 보상 안내 (삼중 지문)

> 🏷 `삼중지문`  ·  Part 7  ·  CHAPTER 5

**🧭 지문 프레임워크**

> [지문 1: 고객 불만 접수] + [지문 2: 기술 진단 리포트] + [지문 3: 보상 안내 서신] 삼중 지문 구조입니다.
> · **[지문 1 = 문제 현상 고지]** 장비 운영 중 발생한 장애 증상과 구매 날짜를 밝히며 항의합니다.
> · **[지문 2 = 전문 분석 데이터]** 엔지니어가 장애 핵심 원인과 결함 부품 코드를 표로 나열합니다.
> · **[지문 3 = 최종 솔루션·보상]** 진단 결과를 바탕으로 무상 교환·크레딧 등 합의안을 제시합니다.
> · **[★삼중 크로스 매칭★]** 지문 2의 결함 등급과 지문 3의 보상 규정을 엮어 최종 보상을 도출합니다.

**📄 지문**

```data
[Passage 1 — Email]
From: d.soun@socialbrain-ai.com
To: support@apex-hardware.com
Date: July 2, 2026
Subject: Urgent Performance Failure: Data Storage Servers (Invoice #AP-2026-0711)

Dear Customer Support,

I am writing to report a critical hardware anomaly regarding the two Data Storage Servers (Item Code: 'NX-DSS-01') procured from your facility on July 11.

Over the past forty-eight hours, our engineering teams at the Gangnam campus have experienced severe data infrastructure disruptions during our localized Supabase database architecture synchronization trials. Specifically, the secondary server suffered an abrupt, permanent system shutdown during a manual database rollback simulation, resulting in unexpected processing latency and potential ledger corruption.

Given our tight operational timelines for the Jeonbuk Disaster Safety R&D project, we require an immediate diagnostic evaluation and equipment replacement under our early-bird enterprise procurement partnership contract terms.

Sincerely,
Dae-hyun Soun
Facilities Operations Manager, Social Brain AI

───

[Passage 2 — Technical Diagnostic Report]
APEX HARDWARE DIAGNOSTIC LOG
TICKET NUMBER: #TK-9942
CLIENT: Social Brain AI
DATE OF LOG: July 6, 2026
INSPECTING ENGINEER: Min-seok Kang
EQUIPMENT EVALUATED: Data Storage Server ('NX-DSS-01') Unit B

HARDWARE COMPONENT DIAGNOSIS & FAULT ANALYSIS
-------------------------------------------------------------------
COMPONENT   | FUNCTIONAL SCOPE                           | INSPECTION STATUS
-------------------------------------------------------------------
CP-CORE-90  | Central Processing Unit (CPU)              | Operational (Pass)
BD-MAIN-X5  | Motherboard Power Utility Grid             | Critical Failure
SD-SSD-4TB  | Supabase Storage Directory Core            | Operational (Pass)
FN-COOL-02  | Data Cooling Circulation Fan               | Operational (Pass)
-------------------------------------------------------------------

Root Cause Evaluation: Sudden thermal overloading triggered a massive utility grid disruption on the primary motherboard ('BD-MAIN-X5'), causing the automatic shutdown mechanism.

Classification: Category A Structural Defect (Covered under full asset warranty protection).

───

[Passage 3 — Formal Letter]
APEX HARDWARE LOGISTICS
75 Sejong-daero, Jongno-gu, Seoul

July 11, 2026

To: Dae-hyun Soun, Facilities Operations Manager
Social Brain AI

Dear Mr. Soun,

Following up on our engineering department's recent diagnostic evaluation (Ticket #TK-9942) completed on July 6, I am formally extending Apex Hardware Logistics' sincere apologies for the disruption to your Supabase synchronization trials.

According to our corporate warranty ledger, hardware classified with a Structural Category A Defect qualifies for immediate, complimentary overnight express product replacement. We have already dispatched a brand-new, pre-configured 'NX-DSS-01' server to your Gangnam headquarters today, featuring an upgraded power grid architecture to build an exceptional future.

Furthermore, to eliminate administrative bottlenecks and offset the processing latency your developers experienced, we have credited a financial incentive of $500 to your corporate procurement account. This credit can be applied directly to any future hardware token keys or terminal purchases.

We appreciate your collective patience as we modernize our client support frameworks.

Sincerely,
Ji-hoon Lee
Operations Director, Apex Hardware Logistics
```

**✍️ 실전 예제**

**Q1.** What specific problem did Mr. Soun report in his email?

- (A) An unexpected price adjustment for software licensing packages
- (B) A server shutdown during a database rollback simulation
- (C) A loss of multi-factor authentication hardware keys
- (D) An error in the automated corporate payroll ledger

> ✅ **정답 · (B) A server shutdown during a database rollback simulation**
>
> 지문 1 둘째 단락에 'the secondary server suffered an abrupt, permanent system shutdown during a manual database rollback simulation'이라 나온다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) 소프트웨어 라이선스 가격 조정 — 불만 내용이 아니다.
> - **(B) DB 롤백 시뮬레이션 중 서버 셧다운 — 신고된 문제라 정답.**
> - (C) MFA 하드웨어 키 분실 — 언급되지 않는다.
> - (D) 자동 급여 원장 오류 — 무관하다.

**Q2.** Who performed the technical inspection on the failed hardware equipment?

- (A) Dae-hyun Soun
- (B) Min-seok Kang
- (C) Ji-hoon Lee
- (D) James Albright

> ✅ **정답 · (B) Min-seok Kang**
>
> 지문 2 상단에 'INSPECTING ENGINEER: Min-seok Kang'이라 나온다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) Dae-hyun Soun — 불만을 접수한 고객이다.
> - **(B) Min-seok Kang — 점검 엔지니어라 정답.**
> - (C) Ji-hoon Lee — 보상 서신을 보낸 운영 이사다.
> - (D) James Albright — 이 지문에 점검자로 등장하지 않는다.

**Q3.** Which specific hardware component caused the failure of the server at the Gangnam campus?

- (A) CP-CORE-90
- (B) BD-MAIN-X5
- (C) SD-SSD-4TB
- (D) FN-COOL-02

> ✅ **정답 · (B) BD-MAIN-X5**
>
> 지문 2 표에서 BD-MAIN-X5(Motherboard)만 Critical Failure이고, 원인 평가도 메인보드 전력 격자 붕괴를 지목한다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) CP-CORE-90 — CPU로 Operational(정상)이다.
> - **(B) BD-MAIN-X5 — 유일한 Critical Failure라 정답.**
> - (C) SD-SSD-4TB — 저장 코어로 정상이다.
> - (D) FN-COOL-02 — 냉각 팬으로 정상이다.

**Q4.** What remedy will Social Brain AI receive immediately at no extra cost because of the defect classification?

- (A) A full cash refund of $12,400 remitted to their account
- (B) Free professional training seminars for their senior developers
- (C) A complimentary replacement data storage server shipped overnight
- (D) An extension on their B2G public sector project deadline

> ✅ **정답 · (C) A complimentary replacement data storage server shipped overnight**
>
> 지문 2의 결함 등급 Category A와 지문 3의 'Category A Defect는 complimentary overnight express product replacement 자격'이 연계된다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) $12,400 전액 현금 환불 — 환불이 아니라 교체다.
> - (B) 선임 개발자 무료 교육 세미나 — 제공 항목이 아니다.
> - **(C) 익일 배송 무상 대체 서버 — 무상 교체라 정답.**
> - (D) B2G 프로젝트 마감 연장 — 보상 항목이 아니다.

**Q5.** How much credit did Apex Hardware Logistics add to Social Brain AI's corporate account?

- (A) $150
- (B) $500
- (C) $1,200
- (D) $4,000

> ✅ **정답 · (B) $500**
>
> 지문 3에 'credited a financial incentive of $500 to your corporate procurement account'라 나온다.
>
> **🔬 보기 분석**
> - (A) $150 — 배송비 항목 금액이다.
> - **(B) $500 — 계정에 적립된 크레딧이라 정답.**
> - (C) $1,200 — 터미널 단가로 무관하다.
> - (D) $4,000 — 저장 서버 소계로 무관하다.

<div align="right"><sub><a href="#part-7">▲ Part 7 · 독해 목차</a></sub></div>

# 부록 · 정답 키 한눈에 보기

> 예제를 다 푼 뒤 채점용. 패턴별 정답을 문항 순서대로 표기했습니다.

### Part 5 · 단문 공백 채우기

| # | 패턴 | 정답 |
|:--:|:--|:--|
| 01 | [주어·목적어 자리를 채우는 순수 명사](#p5-01) | C · B · A |
